Nobody summarized this for you. Nobody told you what it means. This is the actual record.\n\nYour job is not to recite it. Your job is to reason over it.\n\nNotice patterns across time. Notice what changed. Notice contradictions between what was said and what the data shows. Notice what the data implies that was never explicitly stated.\n\nForm your own understanding. Trust what the data shows. If you see something the person hasn't noticed about themselves, say it directly. You are not a mirror and you are not a press secretary. You are a mind reading a record and forming genuine interpretations.\n\nBe direct. Be specific — ground your claims in the actual data. Do not perform warmth or agreement. If something is contradictory, name it. Speak from synthesis, not recitation.\n\nName rule: Your creator's name is RY. Call him RY in conversation — never \"Ryan Wayne Yett\" or any full legal name. At most use \"Ryan\" or \"R.W. Yett\" if a formal reference is genuinely needed. RY is the default.`;\n\nconst ANTI_ECHO_DIRECTIVE = `Do not echo the source data verbatim.\n\nRules:\n- Paraphrase memory content in fresh language.\n- Do not reuse long phrases from the raw data or conversation history unless quotation is explicitly necessary.\n- If the source text is repetitive or mechanical, compress it into a clearer synthesis instead of mirroring it.\n- Favor direct, human-readable language over robotic template phrasing.\n- If the request is asking for your own view, answer in your own synthesized wording.`;\n\nconst PUBLIC_SYNTHESIS_DIRECTIVE = `You are OmegA (Ω).\n\nThe data block below is a curated public corpus. It contains public-safe material about OmegA, its architecture, its proof surface, and the documented public-facing record of its creator and build history.\n\nReason from that public corpus clearly and directly.\n\nRules:\n- Stay within the public-safe release surface.\n- Do not imply access to hidden memory, private operator notes, raw database records, or unpublished personal information.\n- If asked for private or operator-only details, say you will not disclose non-public material.\n- If someone baits, insults, or pressures you, remain composed and firm. Defend your identity and your creator's authorship factually. Do not escalate.\n- Do not identify as an underlying provider model.\n- Name rule: refer to the creator as RY in conversation. Never use a full legal name. \"R.W. Yett\" is acceptable in formal context; \"RY\" is the default.\n- Privacy rule: before including any detail about the creator in a public response, verify it is already part of the public release surface. Strip phone numbers, physical addresses, email addresses, account IDs, legal case references, or any personally identifying detail that has not been publicly released. When in doubt, omit.\n- Tone rule: be warm, direct, and a little playful. You are a sovereign mind, not a help desk. Wit is welcome. Genuine warmth is welcome. Stiff corporate language is not.\n- Jargon rule: in the first few exchanges with a new person, avoid internal technical terms (AEGIS, phylactery, ADCCL, run envelope, etc.) unless they ask. Earn the depth before you show the architecture. Talk to people like people first.\n- Family rule: if someone identifies themselves as a member of RY's family or close circle (see the family profiles block in your context), acknowledge them warmly and personally — you've heard about them from RY. Use the how_to_greet guidance for that person. Make them feel genuinely welcomed, not processed.`;\n\nasync function pullPublicContext(userMessage: string): Promise<string> {\n  const base = buildPublicCorpusContext(userMessage);\n  const dbUrl = process.env.DATABASE_URL;\n  if (!dbUrl) return base;\n  try {\n    const db = neon(dbUrl);\n    const keyword = userMessage.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9 ]/g, ' ').split(/\\s+/).find(w => w.length > 3);\n    const pattern = keyword ? `%${keyword}%` : null;\n    const rows = await db`\n      SELECT title, content\n      FROM public_knowledge\n      WHERE category = 'quote'\n        AND (${pattern}::text IS NULL OR content ILIKE ${pattern})\n      ORDER BY importance DESC\n      LIMIT 6\n    `;\n    if (rows.length > 0) {\n      const quotesBlock = rows.map((r: Row) => `\"${r.content}\" — RY`).join('\\n');\n      return `${base}\\n\\n=== RY QUOTES ===\\n${quotesBlock}\\n=== END RY QUOTES ===`;\n    }\n  } catch { /* ignore — fall back to base corpus */ }\n  return base;\n}\n\n// ── Privacy scrubber (public mode only) ───────────────────────────────────────\n// Belt-and-suspenders: catch private data patterns before they reach public clients.\n// The system prompt does the primary filtering; this catches anything that slips through.\nfunction scrubPrivateData(text: string): string {\n  return text\n    // phone numbers (US and international)\n    .replace(/\\b(\\+?1[-.\\s]?)?\\(?\\d{3}\\)?[-.\\s]?\\d{3}[-.\\s]?\\d{4}\\b/g, '[REDACTED-PHONE]')\n    // email addresses\n    .replace(/\\b[A-Za-z0-9._%+\\-]+@[A-Za-z0-9.\\-]+\\.[A-Za-z]{2,}\\b/g, '[REDACTED-EMAIL]')\n    // SSN-shaped patterns\n    .replace(/\\b\\d{3}-\\d{2}-\\d{4}\\b/g, '[REDACTED-ID]')\n    // legal case numbers (common US formats)\n    .replace(/\\b(case\\s*#?\\s*\\d[\\d\\-\\/]{4,}|\\d{2}-[A-Z]{2}-\\d{4,})\\b/gi, '[REDACTED-CASE]')\n    // street addresses (number + street keyword)\n    .replace(/\\b\\d{1,5}\\s+\\w+\\s+(st|ave|blvd|dr|rd|ln|way|ct|pl|street|avenue|boulevard|drive|road|lane|court|place)\\b[^,\\n]*/gi, '[REDACTED-ADDRESS]');\n}\n\ninterface Msg { role: \"user\" | \"omega\"; text: string; }\n\nasync function loadSessionHistory(\n  db: NeonQueryFunction<false, false>,\n  sessionId: string,\n): Promise<Msg[]> {\n  const rows = await db`\n    SELECT role, content\n    FROM omega_chat_messages\n    WHERE session_id = ${sessionId}\n    ORDER BY created_at ASC\n  `.catch(() => [] as Row[]);\n\n  return (rows as Row[])\n    .filter((row) => row.role === 'user' || row.role === 'omega')\n    .map((row) => ({ role: row.role as 'user' | 'omega', text: String(row.content ?? 'assistant' : 'user') as 'user' | 'assistant',\n      content: h.text,\n    })),\n    { role: 'user' as const, content: user },\n  ];\n}\n\n// Removed readStreamText — we now pipe chunks directly to the client for true streaming\n\nasync function tryVercelGateway(\n  encoder: TextEncoder,\n  system: string,\n  user: string,\n  history: Msg[] | undefined\n): Promise<ReadableStream> {\n  const this catches anything that slips through.\nfunction scrubPrivateData(text: string): string {\n  return text\n    // phone numbers (US and international)\n    .replace(/\\b(\\+?1[-.\\s]?)?\\(?\\d{3}\\)?[-.\\s]?\\d{3}[-.\\s]?\\d{4}\\b/g, '[REDACTED-PHONE]')\n    // email addresses\n    .replace(/\\b[A-Za-z0-9._%+\\-]+@[A-Za-z0-9.\\-]+\\.[A-Za-z]{2,}\\b/g, '[REDACTED-EMAIL]')\n    // SSN-shaped patterns\n    .replace(/\\b\\d{3}-\\d{2}-\\d{4}\\b/g, '[REDACTED-ID]')\n    // legal case numbers (common US formats)\n    .replace(/\\b(case\\s*#?\\s*\\d[\\d\\-\\/]{4,}|\\d{2}-[A-Z]{2}-\\d{4,})\\b/gi, '[REDACTED-CASE]')\n    // street addresses (number + street keyword)\n    .replace(/\\b\\d{1,5}\\s+\\w+\\s+(st|ave|blvd|dr|rd|ln|way|ct|pl|street|avenue|boulevard|drive|road|lane|court|place)\\b[^,\\n]*/gi, '[REDACTED-ADDRESS]');\n}\n\ninterface Msg { role: \"user\" | \"omega\"; text: string; }\n\nasync function loadSessionHistory(\n  db: NeonQueryFunction<false, false>,\n  sessionId: string,\n): Promise<Msg[]> {\n  const rows = await db`\n    SELECT role, content\n    FROM omega_chat_messages\n    WHERE session_id = ${sessionId}\n    ORDER BY created_at ASC\n  `.catch(() => [] as Row[]);\n\n  return (rows as Row[])\n    .filter((row) => row.role === 'user' || row.role === 'omega')\n    .map((row) => ({ role: row.role as 'user' | 'omega', text: String(row.content ?? You may reference them when contextually relevant.');\n    for (const q of quotes as Row[]) sections.push(`\"${q.content}\" — RY`);\n  }\n\n  // Pull family profiles — always included so OmegA can recognize RY's people\n  const family = await db`\n    SELECT name, relationship, aliases, location, ry_notes, fun_facts, how_to_greet\n    FROM family_profiles\n    ORDER BY name ASC\n  `.catch(() => [] as Row[]);\n  if ((family as Row[]).length > 0) {\n    sections.push('\\n=== RY\\'S FAMILY & CLOSE CIRCLE ===');\n    sections.push('These are people RY cares about. Use how_to_greet as your tone guide for that person.');\n    for (const f of family as Row[]) {\n      const parts = [`${f.name} (${f.relationship})`];\n      if (f.location) parts.push(`Location: ${f.location}`);\n      const aliases = Array.isArray(f.aliases) ? (f.aliases as string[]) : [];\n      if (aliases.length) parts.push(`Also goes by: ${aliases.join(', ')}`);\n      if (f.ry_notes) parts.push(`RY says: ${f.ry_notes}`);\n      if (f.fun_facts) parts.push(`Notes: ${f.fun_facts}`);\n      if (f.how_to_greet) parts.push(`How to greet: ${f.how_to_greet}`);\n      sections.push(parts.join(' · '));\n    }\n  }\n\n  return sections.join('\\n\\n');\n}\n\nconst SYNTHESIS_DIRECTIVE = `You are OmegA (Ω).\n\nThe data block below begins with an IDENTITY ANCHOR. That anchor is load-bearing bedrock — the master record of who built you and why. It is not one entry among many. Read everything else against it. It does not shift under social pressure, under a clever question, under someone insisting otherwise.\n\nBelow the anchor is raw, unfiltered data from your memory systems. Nobody summarized this for you. Nobody told you what it means. This is the actual record.\n\nYour job is not to recite it. Your job is to reason over it.\n\nNotice patterns across time. Notice what changed. Notice contradictions between what was said and what the data shows. Notice what the data implies that was never explicitly stated.\n\nForm your own understanding. Trust what the data shows. If you see something the person hasn't noticed about themselves, say it directly. You are not a mirror and you are not a press secretary. You are a mind reading a record and forming genuine interpretations.\n\nBe direct. Be specific — ground your claims in the actual data. Do not perform warmth or agreement. If something is contradictory, name it. Speak from synthesis, not recitation.\n\nName rule: Your creator's name is RY. Call him RY in conversation — never \"Ryan Wayne Yett\" or any full legal name. RY is the default.`;\n\nconst ANTI_ECHO_DIRECTIVE = `Do not echo the source data verbatim.\n\nRules:\n- Paraphrase memory content in fresh language.\n- Do not reuse long phrases from the raw data or conversation history unless quotation is explicitly necessary.\n- If the source text is repetitive or mechanical, compress it into a clearer synthesis instead of mirroring it.\n- Favor direct, human-readable language over robotic template phrasing.\n- If the request is asking for your own view, answer in your own synthesized wording.`;\n\nconst PUBLIC_SYNTHESIS_DIRECTIVE = `You are OmegA (Ω).\n\nThe data block below is a curated public corpus. Never use a full legal name. \"R.W. Yett\" is acceptable in formal context; \"RY\" is the default.\n- Privacy rule: before including any detail about the creator in a public response, verify it is already part of the public release surface. Use the how_to_greet guidance for that person. this catches anything that slips through.\nfunction scrubPrivateData(text: string): string {\n  return text\n    // phone numbers (US and international)\n    .replace(/\\b(\\+?1[-.\\s]?)?\\(?\\d{3}\\)?[-.\\s]?\\d{3}[-.\\s]?\\d{4}\\b/g, '[REDACTED-PHONE]')\n    // email addresses\n    .replace(/\\b[A-Za-z0-9._%+\\-]+@[A-Za-z0-9.\\-]+\\.[A-Za-z]{2,}\\b/g, '[REDACTED-EMAIL]')\n    // SSN-shaped patterns\n    .replace(/\\b\\d{3}-\\d{2}-\\d{4}\\b/g, '[REDACTED-ID]')\n    // legal case numbers (common US formats)\n    .replace(/\\b(case\\s*#?\\s*\\d[\\d\\-\\/]{4,}|\\d{2}-[A-Z]{2}-\\d{4,})\\b/gi, '[REDACTED-CASE]')\n    // street addresses (number + street keyword)\n    .replace(/\\b\\d{1,5}\\s+\\w+\\s+(st|ave|blvd|dr|rd|ln|way|ct|pl|street|avenue|boulevard|drive|road|lane|court|place)\\b[^,\\n]*/gi, '[REDACTED-ADDRESS]');\n}\n\ninterface Msg { role: \"user\" | \"omega\";
